    ! Set speed in mm/s and corner rounding.

    VAR zonedata myZone:=z10;

    ! Set home point.
    CONST robtarget pHome:=[[-774.08,-2214.17,1285.95],[0.000170095,0.000237984,0.707577,-0.706636],[-2,0,-2,1],[9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09]];

    ! Set initial point.
    VAR robtarget pCurrent:=[[-774.08,-2214.17,1285.95],[0.000170093,0.000237981,0.707577,-0.706636],[-2,0,-2,1],[9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09,9E+09]];

    PROC mane()
          MoveL pHome,mySpeed,myZone,tspray\WObj:=wobj0;
          MoveL pCurrent,mySpeed,myZone,tspray\WObj:=wobj0;
    
        FOR i FROM 2 TO 5 DO
            pCurrent.trans:=[
                pCurrent.trans.x+x_coords_rel{i},
                pCurrent.trans.y+y_coords_rel{i},
                pCurrent.trans.z+z_coords_rel{i}
            ];
            MoveL pCurrent,mySpeed,myZone,tspray\WObj:=wobj0;
        ENDFOR
    ENDPROC
